The following actions are running on Node.js 20 and may not work as expected: actions/checkout@v4, actions/setup-java@v4, android-actions/setup-android@v3, gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3. Actions will be forced to run with Node.js 24 by default starting June 2nd, 2026. Please check if updated versions of these actions are available that support Node.js 24.
